Now I see the applyPanelDefaults logic:- If fieldConfig doesn't exist (line 102-106): Create it with empty defaults and overrides- If fieldConfig exists but is malformed (line 109-117):  - If it's a valid map, add missing defaults and overrides  - If defaults key doesn't exist, add it (line 110-111)  - If overrides key doesn't exist, add it (line 113-114)\n\nSo by the time V38 migration runs:\n- All panels should have fieldConfig.defaults and fieldConfig.overrides\n\nBUT! When `fieldConfig[\\\"defaults\\\"]` exists but `fieldConfig[\\\"defaults\\\"][\\\"custom\\\"]` does not (which is the case for dashboards without explicit custom config), the nested conditional on line 117 fails:\\n\\n```go\\nif custom, ok := defaults[\\\"custom\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n```\\n\\nWhen this fails, the entire field config processing block (lines 118-126) is skipped, but more critically, this bypasses the proper initialization of `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` which field overrides depend on for their properties (minWidth, align, displayMode, etc.).\\n\\n**Impact:** While `migrateOverrides()` on line 131 is still called unconditionally, it only processes overrides that explicitly reference \\\"custom.displayMode\\\".
